This starts the Genie-Professor game of chase through time, and causes the Professor to experience different histories as they happen. The Professor, therefore, always starts Puppet History, and the different branches of time always end up here - in this episode. Leviathan? Naphthalim? Ok now I know those nuns were just making this stuff up. I double checked these names just in case, and I was mostly right-- Leviatan is a variation of Leviathan, which is a sea creature mentioned a couple times in the Bible. Naphthalim is the name of one of the twelve original founding fathers of the twelve tribes of Israel. Nothing demon-like about either the sea creature or the person.
